 49 | # Setup log interception
 50 | log_queue = queue.Queue(maxsize=2000)
 51 | 
 52 | class LogQueueHandler(logging.Handler):
 53 |     def emit(self, record):
 54 |         try:
 55 |             msg = self.format(record)
 56 |             log_queue.put_nowait(msg)
 57 |         except Exception:
 58 |             pass
 59 | 
 60 | class StdoutInterceptor:
 61 |     def __init__(self, original_stream):
 62 |         self.original_stream = original_stream
 63 | 
 64 |     def write(self, message):
 65 |         self.original_stream.write(message)
 66 |         if message.strip():
 67 |             try:
 68 |                 log_queue.put_nowait(message.strip())
 69 |             except Exception:
 70 |                 pass
 71 | 
 72 |     def flush(self):
 73 |         self.original_stream.flush()
 74 | 
 75 |     def isatty(self):
 76 |         return hasattr(self.original_stream, 'isatty') and self.original_stream.isatty()
 77 | 
 78 |     def __getattr__(self, name):
 79 |         return getattr(self.original_stream, name)
 80 | 
 81 | # Hook into logging and sys stdout/stderr
 82 | stdout_handler = LogQueueHandler()
 83 | stdout_handler.setFormatter(logging.Formatter('%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s'))
 84 | logging.getLogger().addHandler(stdout_handler)
 85 | 
 86 | sys.stdout = StdoutInterceptor(sys.stdout)
 87 | sys.stderr = StdoutInterceptor(sys.stderr)

125 | # Helper for audio cache hash
126 | def get_audio_cache_path(text: str, voice: str, backend: str, rate: str, pitch: str) -> Path:
127 |     # Clean inputs to avoid weird strings
128 |     key = f"{text.strip()}_{voice.strip()}_{backend.strip()}_{rate.strip()}_{pitch.strip()}"
129 |     h = hashlib.md5(key.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()
130 |     return CACHE_DIR / f"cache_{h}.wav"
131 | 
132 | def get_loaded_whisper(model_name: str = "large-v3-turbo"):
133 |     global whisper_model, current_whisper_model_name
134 |     if WhisperModel is None:
135 |         raise RuntimeError("faster-whisper is not installed on this system.")
136 |     
137 |     with whisper_model_lock:
138 |         if whisper_model is None or current_whisper_model_name != model_name:
139 |             print(f"[SERVER] Loading Whisper model: {model_name}...")
140 |             # Detect device
141 |             device = "cuda" if dubber.torch and dubber.torch.cuda.is_available() else "cpu"
142 |             compute_type = "int8_float16" if device == "cuda" else "int8"
143 |             whisper_model = WhisperModel(model_name, device=device, compute_type=compute_type)
144 |             current_whisper_model_name = model_name
145 |             print(f"[SERVER] Whisper model {model_name} loaded successfully on {device}.")
146 |         return whisper_model
147 | 
148 | def get_ai_engine():
149 |     global ai_engine
150 |     with ai_engine_lock:
151 |         if ai_engine is None:
152 |             print("[SERVER] Instantiating Hy-MT2 AIEngine...")
153 |             ai_engine = dubber.AIEngine(CACHE_DIR)
154 |         return ai_engine

171 |         vram_used = dubber.torch.cuda.memory_allocated(0) / (1024 ** 2) # MB

178 |                 db = json.load(f)
179 |                 num_translations = sum(len(v) for v in db.values())
180 |         except Exception:
181 |             pass
182 |

184 |     total_audio_bytes = sum(f.stat().st_size for f in CACHE_DIR.glob("cache_*.wav"))

188 |         "whisper_model_loaded": whisper_model is not None,
189 |         "whisper_model_name": current_whisper_model_name,

558 | @app.get("/v1/dub_video/download/{job_id}")
559 | def dub_video_download(job_id: str):
560 |     with jobs_lock:
561 |         if job_id not in jobs_state:
562 |             return JSONResponse(status_code=404, content={"error": "Job not found"})
563 |         job = jobs_state[job_id]
564 |         if job["status"] != "completed" or not job["output_file"]:
565 |             return JSONResponse(status_code=400, content={"error": "Job is not completed yet"})

567 |     out_path = Path(job["output_file"])
568 |     if not out_path.exists():
569 |         return JSONResponse(status_code=404, content={"error": "Output file does not exist on disk"})
570 |         
571 |     return FileResponse(out_path, filename=out_path.name, media_type="video/mp4")

 33 | def _transcribe_sync(file_path: str, language: str):
 34 |     """Synchronous transcription worker executed in a background thread."""
 35 |     whisper_lang = None if language.lower() == "auto" else language
 36 |     segments, info = model.transcribe(
 37 |         file_path,
 38 |         beam_size=5,
 39 |         language=whisper_lang,
 40 |         vad_filter=True,
 41 |     )
 42 |     seg_list = list(segments)
 43 |     text = " ".join(seg.text for seg in seg_list).strip()
 44 |     return info, text, seg_list
 45 | 
 46 | 
 47 | @app.post("/v1/audio/transcriptions")
 48 | async def transcribe(
 49 |     file: UploadFile = File(...),
 50 |     model: str = Form(DEFAULT_MODEL_NAME),   # kept for compatibility with caller
 51 |     language: str = Form("auto"),
 52 |     response_format: str = Form("json"),
 53 | ):
 54 |     """
 55 |     OpenAI-like transcription endpoint (memory-safe & non-blocking).
 56 |     """
 57 |     # Write incoming file to a temporary file in chunks to avoid memory bloat
 58 |     with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(delete=False, suffix=".wav") as tmp:
 59 |         while True:
 60 |             chunk = await file.read(8192)
 61 |             if not chunk:
 62 |                 break
 63 |             tmp.write(chunk)
 64 |         tmp_path = tmp.name
 65 | 
 66 |     try:
 67 |         # Offload CPU/GPU bound task to prevent blocking the event loop
 68 |         info, text, seg_list = await asyncio.to_thread(_transcribe_sync, tmp_path, language)
 69 |     finally:
 70 |         if os.path.exists(tmp_path):
 71 |             os.remove(tmp_path)
 72 | 
 73 |     if response_format == "json":
 74 |         return JSONResponse(
 75 |             {
 76 |                 "language": info.language,
 77 |                 "text": text,
 78 |                 "segments": [
 79 |                     {
 80 |                         "id": i,
 81 |                         "start": seg.start,
 82 |                         "end": seg.end,
 83 |                         "text": seg.text,
 84 |                     }
 85 |                     for i, seg in enumerate(seg_list)
 86 |                 ],
 87 |             }
 88 |         )
 89 |     else:
 90 |         return text
 91 |

 93 | if __name__ == "__main__":
 94 |     uvicorn.run(
 95 |         app,
 96 |         host="0.0.0.0",

 49 | # Setup log interception
 50 | log_queue = queue.Queue(maxsize=2000)
 51 | 
 52 | class LogQueueHandler(logging.Handler):
 53 |     def emit(self, record):
 54 |         try:
 55 |             msg = self.format(record)
 56 |             log_queue.put_nowait(msg)
 57 |         except Exception:
 58 |             pass
 59 | 
 60 | class StdoutInterceptor:
 61 |     def __init__(self, original_stream):
 62 |         self.original_stream = original_stream
 63 | 
 64 |     def write(self, message):
 65 |         self.original_stream.write(message)
 66 |         if message.strip():
 67 |             try:
 68 |                 log_queue.put_nowait(message.strip())
 69 |             except Exception:
 70 |                 pass
 71 | 
 72 |     def flush(self):
 73 |         self.original_stream.flush()
 74 | 
 75 |     def isatty(self):
 76 |         return hasattr(self.original_stream, 'isatty') and self.original_stream.isatty()
 77 | 
 78 |     def __getattr__(self, name):
 79 |         return getattr(self.original_stream, name)
 80 | 
 81 | # Hook into logging and sys stdout/stderr
 82 | stdout_handler = LogQueueHandler()
 83 | stdout_handler.setFormatter(logging.Formatter('%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s'))
 84 | logging.getLogger().addHandler(stdout_handler)
 85 | 
 86 | sys.stdout = StdoutInterceptor(sys.stdout)
 87 | sys.stderr = StdoutInterceptor(sys.stderr)

**Assistant:**



Ah! Let's examine:
Both `whisper_server.py` and `dubbing_server.py` are run on port 9000 by default!
- `whisper_server.py` runs on port 9000.
- `dubbing_server.py` runs on port 9000.
- Also, `dubber.py` tries to reach `whisper_server` at `http://127.0.0.1:9000/v1/audio/transcriptions`.
Wait, if `dubbing_server.py` and `whisper_server.py` both try to run on port 9000, they will conflict.
In `dubbing_server.py`, let's see how they start or locate it. If we run `dubbing_server.py` on port 9000, then we should run `whisper_server.py` on port 9001! Or vice-versa. Let's look at `dubbing_server.py` line 724:
`port: int = 9000`
`whisper_url: str = "http://127.0.0.1:9001"` -> Wait, where was that? It says in `AUDIT_REALTIME_DUBBING.md`:
```
host: str = "127.0.0.1"
port: int = 9000
whisper_url: str = "http://127.0.0.1:9001"
```
So we can run `whisper_server.py` on port `9001`, and `dubbing_server.py` on port `9000`!
Wait, let's verify what `dubber.py` has for `WHISPER_SERVER_URL`:
`WHISPER_SERVER_URL = "http://127.0.0.1:9000/v1/audio/transcriptions"` (line 153). And around line 1608:
```python
    whisper_port = 9000
```
Let's see: if we change `whisper_server.py` to run on port `9001` and update `dubber.py` and any other references to point to `http://127.0.0.1:9001/v1/audio/transcriptions` and `whisper_port = 9001`, that will perfectly solve the duplicate port conflict!
Let's search for `whisper_port` in `dubber.py` to see all references to port 9000 for whisper.

Ah, in `dubber.py` line 1637, there is a `shell=True` subprocess call starting WSL! Let's address all of these critical vulnerabilities.

Let's break down the plan for **Phase 3: Realtime Dubbing Critical Fixes**:
1. **C1: Fix duplicate port binding**: Change `whisper_server.py` default port from `9000` to `9001` (to prevent conflict with `dubbing_server.py` running on `9000`). Update references to port 9000 for whisper server in `dubber.py`, `dubbing_server.py`, and `whisper_server.py` to `9001`.
2. **C2: API key authentication**: Let's add API key auth (from a `.env` file, or fallback to a default secure autogenerated key/token or environment variable) to all FastAPI endpoints in `dubbing_server.py` and `whisper_server.py`. Let's support an `X-API-Key` header and `api_key` query param.
3. **C3: Upload file validation**: In both `dubbing_server.py` and `whisper_server.py`, validate uploads. Let's restrict file sizes to e.g., 500MB (fully configurable), restrict extensions (e.g., audio/video formats: wav, mp3, mp4, mkv, avi, webm, srt), and validate Content-Type.
4. **C4: Replace shell=True / unsafe subprocess**: In `dubber.py`, around line 1637, replace `subprocess.Popen(..., shell=True)` with a list of arguments and no shell, or structure it safely to avoid command injection. Wait, on Windows, starting WSL via `wsl.exe` directly is extremely easy and doesn't require a shell!
Let's see: `cmd = ["wsl", "bash", "-ic", "cd ~/OmniVoice && source .venv/bin/activate && omnivoice-triton-server start --port 8889"]` - we can run this directly using `subprocess.Popen` with `creationflags=CREATE_NEW_CONSOLE` and NO `shell=True`! This is incredibly elegant and far more secure!
5. **C5: Race conditions in model swapping and translation DB**:
   - For `current_whisper_model_name`, use thread locks (actually `asyncio.Lock` since these are async FastAPI servers!).
   - Wait, `dubbing_server.py` uses `whisper_model_lock = threading.Lock()` and then does `get_loaded_whisper(model_name)` which can block. Let's make it more robust.
   - For `TRANSLATION_DB_PATH` reading and writing, it's a JSON file. If multiple requests read/write it at the same time, it can get corrupted! Let's add a robust lock (`threading.Lock` / file lock / write-to-temp-then-rename) when reading/writing to ensure no corruption.
6. **C6: Hardcoded cuda device in whisper_server**:
   Let's check `whisper_server.py` line 18:
   `model = WhisperModel(DEFAULT_MODEL_NAME, device="cuda", compute_type="int8_float16")`
   If the machine does not have a CUDA GPU, this will fail instantly!
   Let's dynamically detect if a CUDA GPU is available using `torch.cuda.is_available()`. If torch is not available, we can try to load CUDA, and fallback to CPU and `compute_type="int8"` automatically! That makes it 100% robust.
7. **C7: Memory/Disk bounds**:
   - Clear job state TTL: currently, `jobs_state = {}` grows forever. Let's prune job states older than 24 hours.
   - Cache eviction: `ttscache_local` can grow infinitely. Let's implement a simple LRU or maximum size/count cache eviction policy (e.g., prune oldest files if total size > 1GB or count > 500).
8. **C8: Replace print with structured logging**:
   Let's configure a standard logging mechanism with timestamps, log levels, and write them to a log file, while keeping the StdoutInterceptor queue functioning perfectly.

Let's begin editing!

Awesome. Let's look at `../Realtime Dubbing/dubber.py` and see where else it does subprocess calls to make sure they are safe, or if they are already list-based. We see from the search that they are indeed list-based:
- `subprocess.run(cmd, ...)` (lines 329, 368)

Let's read `dubber.py` around lines 1625 to 1648 to see the exact context for starting OmniVoice.
Wait, let's also make sure we understand the WSL launch.
Instead of:
```python
wsl_command = 'wsl bash -ic "cd ~/OmniVoice && source .venv/bin/activate && omnivoice-triton-server start --port 8889"'
subprocess.Popen(
    f'cmd.exe /c start "OmniVoice Triton (WSL)" {wsl_command}',
    shell=True
)
```
We can run:
```python
subprocess.Popen(
    ["cmd.exe", "/c", "start", "OmniVoice Triton (WSL)", "wsl", "bash", "-ic", "cd ~/OmniVoice && source .venv/bin/activate && omnivoice-triton-server start --port 8889"],
    creationflags=creationflags
)
```
Wait, using a list of arguments for `subprocess.Popen` when spawning a terminal window on Windows with `start` works beautifully and avoids any shell parsing/injection! Let's verify:
Is `cmd.exe` a safe command when invoked as list on Windows? Yes, calling executable list arguments natively handles parameter escaping and does not invoke the Windows command shell runner (`shell=True`), making it immune to command injection.

Let's first edit `whisper_server.py` to fix:
1. Hardcoded cuda device: use dynamic detection of cuda device (C6).
2. Use structured logging (C8).
3. Add port customizability or default to `9001` (C1).
4. Add API Key authentication (C2).
5. Add file upload validation (C3).

Wait, let's look at `whisper_server.py` line 1-30. Let's read lines 1-40 again to make sure we make precise edits. We already have the content:
```python
import io
import os
import tempfile
import asyncio

from fastapi import FastAPI, File, UploadFile, Form
from fastapi.exceptions import RequestValidationError
from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse
from faster_whisper import WhisperModel
import uvicorn
```
Let's see: how can we dynamically check for cuda?
We can import `torch` or check using `faster_whisper` device detection, or we can use `torch` if it is installed, or try-except faster_whisper loading. Actually, `faster-whisper` itself raises an exception if CUDA is requested but not available. We can do:
```python
# Detect device dynamically
device = "cuda"
compute_type = "int8_float16"
try:
    import torch
    if not torch.cuda.is_available():
        device = "cpu"
        compute_type = "int8"
except ImportError:
    # Fallback try-catch on model creation or check if CUDA is installed
    pass
```
Wait, we can wrap the model loading inside a helper or try-except:
```python
try:
    print(f"[SERVER] Loading Whisper model on device={device} with compute_type={compute_type}...")
    model = WhisperModel(DEFAULT_MODEL_NAME, device=device, compute_type=compute_type)
except Exception as e:
    print(f"[SERVER] Failed to load on CUDA, falling back to CPU: {e}")
    device = "cpu"
    compute_type = "int8"
    model = WhisperModel(DEFAULT_MODEL_NAME, device=device, compute_type=compute_type)
```
This is extremely robust! It handles any scenario: CUDA not available, driver mismatch, or library path issues.

Let's look at API Key Authentication. We can implement a simple API key check. Let's read the API Key from `DUBBING_API_KEY` env var or fallback to a default secure key if not set (or we can read it from a shared config / env file).
Wait, we have a `.env` in `Computer-Use` (which is the current directory). Let's see if we can read the environment variables using `python-dotenv` if installed, or standard `os.environ`.
Let's load dotenv in `whisper_server.py`:
```python
try:
    from dotenv import load_dotenv
    load_dotenv()
except ImportError:
    pass
```
And check:
```python
API_KEY = os.environ.get("DUBBING_API_KEY", "default_secure_dubbing_key_123")
```
We can write a FastAPI dependency `verify_api_key`:
```python
from fastapi import Security, HTTPException, status
from fastapi.security.api_key import APIKeyHeader, APIKeyQuery

api_key_header = APIKeyHeader(name="X-API-Key", auto_error=False)
api_key_query = APIKeyQuery(name="api_key", auto_error=False)

def verify_api_key(
    key_header: str = Security(api_key_header),
    key_query: str = Security(api_key_query)
):
    if not API_KEY:
        return  # Auth disabled if API_KEY is empty
    if key_header == API_KEY or key_query == API_KEY:
        return
    raise HTTPException(
        status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
        detail="Invalid or missing API key."
    )
```
Then we can add `dependencies=[Depends(verify_api_key)]` to the endpoints or to the entire FastAPI app (except `/health`). Adding it as a global or route-specific dependency is perfect!
Wait, `/health` should remain unauthenticated so that orchestrators can perform health checks.

Let's look at Upload File Validation (C3).
For transcribing:
```python
    file: UploadFile = File(...),
```
We can validate:
- Size: reading chunks and counting bytes. If the total bytes exceed the maximum size (e.g. 500MB), raise a 413 Payload Too Large exception.
- Extension: extract the extension of `file.filename` and check if it is in an allowed set (e.g., `[".wav", ".mp3", ".m4a", ".flac", ".ogg", ".mp4", ".mkv", ".avi", ".webm", ".mov"]`).
- Content-Type: check if it starts with `audio/` or `video/` or matches a list of audio/video content-types, but fallback gracefully.
Let's implement a robust validator helper:
```python
ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS = {".wav", ".mp3", ".m4a", ".flac", ".ogg", ".mp4", ".mkv", ".avi", ".webm", ".mov"}
MAX_FILE_SIZE = 500 * 1024 * 1024  # 500 MB

def validate_uploaded_file(file: UploadFile):
    # Validate Extension
    filename = file.filename or ""
    _, ext = os.path.splitext(filename.lower())
    if ext not in ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS:
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,
            detail=f"File extension '{ext}' is not allowed. Supported formats: {', '.join(ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS)}"
        )
    
    # Validate Content-Type
    content_type = file.content_type or ""
    if not (content_type.startswith("audio/") or content_type.startswith("video/") or content_type == "application/octet-stream"):
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,
            detail="Invalid content type. Only audio and video files are supported."
        )
```
And to validate file size without reading everything into memory, we can read chunks:
```python
    total_size = 0
    with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(delete=False, suffix=ext) as tmp:
        while True:
            chunk = await file.read(1024 * 1024)  # 1MB chunks
            if not chunk:
                break
            total_size += len(chunk)
            if total_size > MAX_FILE_SIZE:
                tmp.close()
                if os.path.exists(tmp.name):
                    os.remove(tmp.name)
                raise HTTPException(
                    status_code=status.HTTP_413_PAYLOAD_TOO_LARGE,
                    detail=f"File size exceeds the limit of {MAX_FILE_SIZE // (1024 * 1024)}MB."
                )
            tmp.write(chunk)
        tmp_path = tmp.name
```
This is extremely clean, memory-safe, and secure! Let's implement this validation in both `whisper_server.py` and `dubbing_server.py`.

Let's modify `whisper_server.py` with these enhancements. Let's first read the entire file of `whisper_server.py` so we don't miss anything. It's only 100 lines long! Let's read lines 41 to 100 of `whisper_server.py`.

**Assistant:**



Let's rewrite `../Realtime Dubbing/whisper_server.py` using `write_to_file`. It's only 100 lines, so rewriting it with clean, robust, and commented code is safe and highly efficient.
Wait! Let's carefully handle imports and make sure we don't break anything.
We'll include:
- API key check dependency.
- Dynamic CUDA detection try-except fallback.
- Standard logging.
- Support default port 9001 (configurable via environment `WHISPER_PORT` or CLI args, fallback to 9001).
- File size, extension, and content-type validation.
Let's prepare the code:

```python
import io
import os
import sys
import logging
import tempfile
import asyncio
from pathlib import Path

from fastapi import FastAPI, File, UploadFile, Form, HTTPException, Security, status, Depends
from fastapi.exceptions import RequestValidationError
from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse
from fastapi.security import APIKeyHeader, APIKeyQuery
from faster_whisper import WhisperModel
import uvicorn

# Setup structured logging
logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s [%(levelname)s] %(name)s: %(message)s",
    handlers=[
        logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout),
        logging.FileHandler("whisper_server.log", encoding="utf-8")
    ]
)
logger = logging.getLogger("whisper_server")

try:
    from dotenv import load_dotenv
    load_dotenv()
except ImportError:
    pass

app = FastAPI(title="Whisper ASR Server", version="1.0.0")

# Security configuration
API_KEY = os.environ.get("DUBBING_API_KEY", "default_secure_dubbing_key_123")
api_key_header = APIKeyHeader(name="X-API-Key", auto_error=False)
api_key_query = APIKeyQuery(name="api_key", auto_error=False)

def verify_api_key(
    key_header: str = Security(api_key_header),
    key_query: str = Security(api_key_query)
):
    if not API_KEY:
        return
    if key_header == API_KEY or key_query == API_KEY:
        return
    raise HTTPException(
        status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
        detail="Invalid or missing API key."
    )

DEFAULT_MODEL_NAME = "large-v3-turbo"

# Dynamic device and compute type detection
device = "cuda"
compute_type = "int8_float16"

try:
    import torch
    if not torch.cuda.is_available():
        device = "cpu"
        compute_type = "int8"
except ImportError:
    pass

logger.info(f"Loading Whisper model: '{DEFAULT_MODEL_NAME}' on device='{device}' (compute_type='{compute_type}')...")
try:
    model = WhisperModel(DEFAULT_MODEL_NAME, device=device, compute_type=compute_type)
    logger.info("Model loaded successfully.")
except Exception as e:
    logger.warning(f"Failed to load Whisper on {device} with compute_type={compute_type}: {e}")
    if device == "cuda":
        logger.info("Falling back to CPU...")
        device = "cpu"
        compute_type = "int8"
        model = WhisperModel(DEFAULT_MODEL_NAME, device=device, compute_type=compute_type)
        logger.info("Model loaded successfully on CPU.")
    else:
        raise e

@app.exception_handler(RequestValidationError)
async def validation_exception_handler(request, exc):
    logger.error(f"422 validation error: {exc.errors()}")
    return JSONResponse(status_code=422, content={"detail": exc.errors()})

@app.get("/health")
def health():
    return {"status": "ok", "device": device, "compute_type": compute_type}

def _transcribe_sync(file_path: str, language: str):
    """Synchronous transcription worker executed in a background thread."""
    whisper_lang = None if language.lower() == "auto" else language
    segments, info = model.transcribe(
        file_path,
        beam_size=5,
        language=whisper_lang,
        vad_filter=True,
    )
    seg_list = list(segments)
    text = " ".join(seg.text for seg in seg_list).strip()
    return info, text, seg_list

# Allowed Extensions and size limit
ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS = {".wav", ".mp3", ".m4a", ".flac", ".ogg", ".mp4", ".mkv", ".avi", ".webm", ".mov"}
MAX_FILE_SIZE = 500 * 1024 * 1024  # 500 MB

@app.post("/v1/audio/transcriptions")
async def transcribe(
    file: UploadFile = File(...),
    model_name: str = Form(DEFAULT_MODEL_NAME),
    language: str = Form("auto"),
    response_format: str = Form("json"),
    authenticated: None = Depends(verify_api_key)
):
    """
    OpenAI-like transcription endpoint (memory-safe, validated, non-blocking).
    """
    filename = file.filename or "audio.wav"
    _, ext = os.path.splitext(filename.lower())
    if ext not in ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS:
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,
            detail=f"File extension '{ext}' is not allowed. Supported formats: {', '.join(ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS)}"
        )

    content_type = file.content_type or ""
    if not (content_type.startswith("audio/") or content_type.startswith("video/") or content_type == "application/octet-stream"):
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,
            detail="Invalid content type. Only audio and video files are supported."
        )

    # Write incoming file to temporary file with size validation
    total_size = 0
    with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(delete=False, suffix=ext) as tmp:
        try:
            while True:
                chunk = await file.read(1024 * 1024)  # 1MB chunks
                if not chunk:
                    break
                total_size += len(chunk)
                if total_size > MAX_FILE_SIZE:
                    raise HTTPException(
                        status_code=status.HTTP_413_PAYLOAD_TOO_LARGE,
                        detail=f"File size exceeds limit of {MAX_FILE_SIZE // (1024 * 1024)}MB."
                    )
                tmp.write(chunk)
            tmp_path = tmp.name
        except Exception as e:
            tmp.close()
            if os.path.exists(tmp.name):
                os.remove(tmp.name)
            raise e

    try:
        # Offload GPU-bound task to prevent blocking the event loop
        info, text, seg_list = await asyncio.to_thread(_transcribe_sync, tmp_path, language)
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"ASR error during transcription: {e}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"ASR processing failed: {e}")
    finally:
        if os.path.exists(tmp_path):
            try:
                os.remove(tmp_path)
            except Exception as e:
                logger.warning(f"Failed to remove temp file {tmp_path}: {e}")

    if response_format == "json":
        return JSONResponse(
            {
                "language": info.language,
                "text": text,
                "segments": [
                    {
                        "id": i,
                        "start": seg.start,
                        "end": seg.end,
                        "text": seg.text,
                    }
                    for i, seg in enumerate(seg_list)
                ],
            }
        )
    else:
        return Response(content=text, media_type="text/plain")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    # Defaulting to 9001 to avoid duplicate port conflict on 9000
    port = int(os.environ.get("WHISPER_PORT", 9001))
    uvicorn.run(
        app,
        host="0.0.0.0",
        port=port,
        log_level="info",
        reload=False,
    )
```

This is absolutely gorgeous, fully production-grade, and beautifully secure! Let's write this to `../Realtime Dubbing/whisper_server.py`.

Path: ../Realtime Dubbing/whisper_server.py
Content: import io
import os
import sys
import logging
import tempfile
import asyncio
from pathlib import Path

from fastapi import FastAPI, File, UploadFile, Form, HTTPException, Security, status, Depends
from fastapi.exceptions import RequestValidationError
from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse
from fastapi.security import APIKeyHeader, APIKeyQuery
from faster_whisper import WhisperModel
import uvicorn

# Setup structured logging
logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format="%(asctime)s [%(levelname)s] %(name)s: %(message)s",
    handlers=[
        logging.StreamHandler(sys.stdout),
        logging.FileHandler("whisper_server.log", encoding="utf-8")
    ]
)
logger = logging.getLogger("whisper_server")

try:
    from dotenv import load_dotenv
    load_dotenv()
except ImportError:
    pass

app = FastAPI(title="Whisper ASR Server", version="1.0.0")

# Security configuration
API_KEY = os.environ.get("DUBBING_API_KEY", "default_secure_dubbing_key_123")
api_key_header = APIKeyHeader(name="X-API-Key", auto_error=False)
api_key_query = APIKeyQuery(name="api_key", auto_error=False)

def verify_api_key(
    key_header: str = Security(api_key_header),
    key_query: str = Security(api_key_query)
):
    if not API_KEY:
        return
    if key_header == API_KEY or key_query == API_KEY:
        return
    raise HTTPException(
        status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
        detail="Invalid or missing API key."
    )

DEFAULT_MODEL_NAME = "large-v3-turbo"

# Dynamic device and compute type detection
device = "cuda"
compute_type = "int8_float16"

try:
    import torch
    if not torch.cuda.is_available():
        device = "cpu"
        compute_type = "int8"
except ImportError:
    pass

logger.info(f"Loading Whisper model: '{DEFAULT_MODEL_NAME}' on device='{device}' (compute_type='{compute_type}')...")
try:
    model = WhisperModel(DEFAULT_MODEL_NAME, device=device, compute_type=compute_type)
    logger.info("Model loaded successfully.")
except Exception as e:
    logger.warning(f"Failed to load Whisper on {device} with compute_type={compute_type}: {e}")
    if device == "cuda":
        logger.info("Falling back to CPU...")
        device = "cpu"
        compute_type = "int8"
        model = WhisperModel(DEFAULT_MODEL_NAME, device=device, compute_type=compute_type)
        logger.info("Model loaded successfully on CPU.")
    else:
        raise e

@app.exception_handler(RequestValidationError)
async def validation_exception_handler(request, exc):
    logger.error(f"422 validation error: {exc.errors()}")
    return JSONResponse(status_code=422, content={"detail": exc.errors()})

@app.get("/health")
def health():
    return {"status": "ok", "device": device, "compute_type": compute_type}

def _transcribe_sync(file_path: str, language: str):
    """Synchronous transcription worker executed in a background thread."""
    whisper_lang = None if language.lower() == "auto" else language
    segments, info = model.transcribe(
        file_path,
        beam_size=5,
        language=whisper_lang,
        vad_filter=True,
    )
    seg_list = list(segments)
    text = " ".join(seg.text for seg in seg_list).strip()
    return info, text, seg_list

# Allowed Extensions and size limit
ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS = {".wav", ".mp3", ".m4a", ".flac", ".ogg", ".mp4", ".mkv", ".avi", ".webm", ".mov"}
MAX_FILE_SIZE = 500 * 1024 * 1024  # 500 MB

@app.post("/v1/audio/transcriptions")
async def transcribe(
    file: UploadFile = File(...),
    model_name: str = Form(DEFAULT_MODEL_NAME),
    language: str = Form("auto"),
    response_format: str = Form("json"),
    authenticated: None = Depends(verify_api_key)
):
    """
    OpenAI-like transcription endpoint (memory-safe, validated, non-blocking).
    """
    filename = file.filename or "audio.wav"
    _, ext = os.path.splitext(filename.lower())
    if ext not in ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS:
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,
            detail=f"File extension '{ext}' is not allowed. Supported formats: {', '.join(ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS)}"
        )

    content_type = file.content_type or ""
    if not (content_type.startswith("audio/") or content_type.startswith("video/") or content_type == "application/octet-stream"):
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,
            detail="Invalid content type. Only audio and video files are supported."
        )

    # Write incoming file to temporary file with size validation
    total_size = 0
    with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(delete=False, suffix=ext) as tmp:
        try:
            while True:
                chunk = await file.read(1024 * 1024)  # 1MB chunks
                if not chunk:
                    break
                total_size += len(chunk)
                if total_size > MAX_FILE_SIZE:
                    raise HTTPException(
                        status_code=status.HTTP_413_PAYLOAD_TOO_LARGE,
                        detail=f"File size exceeds limit of {MAX_FILE_SIZE // (1024 * 1024)}MB."
                    )
                tmp.write(chunk)
            tmp_path = tmp.name
        except Exception as e:
            tmp.close()
            if os.path.exists(tmp.name):
                os.remove(tmp.name)
            raise e

    try:
        # Offload GPU-bound task to prevent blocking the event loop
        info, text, seg_list = await asyncio.to_thread(_transcribe_sync, tmp_path, language)
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"ASR error during transcription: {e}")
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=f"ASR processing failed: {e}")
    finally:
        if os.path.exists(tmp_path):
            try:
                os.remove(tmp_path)
            except Exception as e:
                logger.warning(f"Failed to remove temp file {tmp_path}: {e}")

    if response_format == "json":
        return JSONResponse(
            {
                "language": info.language,
                "text": text,
                "segments": [
                    {
                        "id": i,
                        "start": seg.start,
                        "end": seg.end,
                        "text": seg.text,
                    }
                    for i, seg in enumerate(seg_list)
                ],
            }
        )
    else:
        return Response(content=text, media_type="text/plain")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    # Defaulting to 9001 to avoid duplicate port conflict on 9000
    port = int(os.environ.get("WHISPER_PORT", 9001))
    uvicorn.run(
        app,
        host="0.0.0.0",
        port=port,
        log_level="info",
        reload=False,
    )

**Assistant:**



We see that `requests.post` is called with:
```python
resp = requests.post(WHISPER_SERVER_URL, files=files, data=data, timeout=None)
```
Let's see: we should pass the API Key if `DUBBING_API_KEY` is set!
Let's define a helper in `dubber.py` or just construct a headers dict:
```python
def get_whisper_headers():
    key = os.environ.get("DUBBING_API_KEY", "default_secure_dubbing_key_123")
    if key:
        return {"X-API-Key": key}
    return {}
```
This is brilliant! We can use `get_whisper_headers()` for any post requests to `WHISPER_SERVER_URL`.
Let's find other `requests.post` in `dubber.py`. We saw three locations:
1. Line 500: `resp = requests.post(WHISPER_SERVER_URL, files=files, data=data, timeout=None)`
2. Line 571: `resp = requests.post(WHISPER_SERVER_URL, files=files, data=data, timeout=None)`
3. Line 1271: `resp = requests.post(WHISPER_SERVER_URL, files=files, data=data)`
